## Summary: Noted Terminal Architecture & Features

I have successfully reviewed all the specified knowledge files and feature documentation. Here are the key findings organized by your questions:

---

### 1. **AI Research/Chat Integration (Gemini)**

**File: `/Users/fedor/Desktop/custom-terminal/docs/features/research.md`**

**How It Works:**
- **Activation:** Users trigger AI research via context menu (right-click on selected text) → "Research Selection" or by clicking **"Буфер"** (Buffer) button in the Gemini panel
- **Modes:**
  - `🔍 Research`: Uses `gemini-2.0-flash` (standard inference)
  - `📋 Compact`: Uses `gemini-3-flash` with Thinking: HIGH mode
  - Google Search tools auto-activate for gemini-3 models
- **UI Flow:** 
  1. Content triggers `pendingResearch` flag in `useResearchStore`
  2. Right panel (InfoPanel) switches to **AI** tab automatically
  3. Loading spinners appear in chat list
  4. Markdown response renders with inline code support
  5. Users can **Retry** (remove tail, resend) or **Delete** messages

**Session Capture (Sniper 2.0):**
- **File:** `knowledge/fix-gemini-id-capture.md`
- Gemini creates session files lazily (`session-*.json` in `~/.gemini/tmp/<hash>/chats/`)
- Path hashing: SHA256 of terminal's CWD determines folder
- Long-lived Watcher (5 min timeout) watches for file creation
- Upon detection: Parse JSON to extract full UUID
- Watcher attached to tab lifecycle (`gemini:close-watcher`)

**Session Forking (True Fork):**
- **File:** `knowledge/fix-gemini-true-fork.md`
- Simple `-r <sessionId>` resume doesn't work for branching
- True fork requires:
  1. Find original `session-*.json` by UUID
  2. Copy file under new name
  3. **Patch JSON:** Update `sessionId` field inside (critical—Gemini validates filename vs internal ID match)
  4. Launch new CLI copy with new UUID

---

### 2. **Copy Session / Clean Export**

**File: `/Users/fedor/Desktop/custom-terminal/docs/knowledge/fix-claude-clean-export.md`**

**The Problem:**
- Raw Claude Code `.jsonl` files contain massive `tool_result` outputs (file reads, edits, diffs)
- Direct export fills AI context window with useless data

**Solution: Intelligent Filtering (IPC: `claude:export-clean-session`):**
- **User Messages:** Only text prompt preserved; `tool_result` completely removed
- **Assistant Messages:** Keep response text + `thinking` blocks (capped at 500 chars)
- **Actions:** Replace embedded code with compact emoji-labels:
  - `📄 Reading (/path/to/file)`
  - `✏️ Editing (/path/to/file)`  
  - `🖥 Command ("ls -la")`
- **Result:** 5000+ line session → 50-100 line Markdown with full logic intact

**Multi-Tab Selection:**
- **File:** `knowledge/fact-selection-model.md`
- State: `selectedTabIds` array in workspace store
- Interactions: `Shift+Click` (range), `Cmd+Click` (individual), normal click (reset)
- Bulk actions: "Copy X Sessions" button, adapted context menu
- **Critical rule:** Color indicator (`borderTop`) shows ONLY on active tab, even if multiple selected

---

### 3. **Notes System**

**File: `/Users/fedor/Desktop/custom-terminal/docs/features/notes.md`**

**Workflow:**
1. **Quick capture:** Type in "Project Notes" field on Info panel → auto-saves on blur or `Cmd+Enter`
2. **Full editor:** `Cmd+E` → floating sheet with Markdown editor
3. **Editing:** Autofocus on open, supports Markdown syntax, supports CodeMirror
4. **Saving:** Auto-save on close (`Esc`/`Cmd+E`) or manual `Cmd+S`
5. **Sync:** Changes reflect instantly across all UI components

**Technical Details:**
- **Binding:** Per-project (`projectId` based)
- **Storage:** SQLite + JSON (see persistence patterns below)
- **Mode:** Full-screen uses `z-index: 50` overlay
- **Scrolling:** Fixed via `min-h-0` + CodeMirror `overflow-x: hidden`

**Key Fix (fix-markdown-editor-recreation.md):**
- Avoid literal array defaults in destructuring: `{ includeOffsets = [] }` causes re-creation
- Solution: Use module-level stable constant + `useEffect` dependency on stable reference

---

### 4. **System Prompts Configuration**

**Not explicitly documented in the read files.** However, I found these relevant patterns:

- **Command Type Persistence:** `command_type` stored in SQLite `tabs` table (see `fix-tab-rename-on-restart.md`)
- **State-driven triggers:** InfoPanel responds to `geminiSessionId`, `claudeSessionId`, `pendingResearch` flags
- **Session recovery:** `wasInterrupted` + `overlayDismissed` flags manage overlay behavior (see next section)

---

### 5. **InfoPanel & AI UI Flicker Fix**

**File: `/Users/fedor/Desktop/custom-terminal/docs/knowledge/fix-ai-ui-flicker.md`**

**The Problem:**
- During Rollback/Fork, right panel briefly (300-500ms) shows "No active session"
- Root: `closeTab()` zeroes `geminiSessionId`, then `createTab()` creates empty tab, then sniper watcher eventually injects ID

**Solution: Immediate Injection**
- Pass `geminiSessionId`/`claudeSessionId` directly in `createTab(options)`
- Tab created **with** ID already set
- InfoPanel sees ID instantly, no flicker
- Sniper watcher not needed for restored tabs—ID comes from SQLite

**InfoPanel Tabs:**
- Tab 1: **Utilities** (Scripts, Logs, Logs Compression)
- Tab 2: **AI** (Gemini Research + Claude session controls)
- Tab 3: **Notes** (Project documentation)
- Tab 4: **Timeline** (Claude history navigation with Backtrace algorithm)

**Interrupted Overlay Persistence (fix-interrupted-overlay-persistence.md):**
- Flags: `wasInterrupted` + `overlayDismissed`
- When new AI session starts: Both flags reset to `false`
- On app close: `beforeunload` → `markAllSessionsInterrupted()` sets `wasInterrupted=true` (if `!overlayDismissed`)
- User can dismiss or continue—choice persists until next session launch

---

### 6. **Relevant Patterns for AI-Powered Features**

**A. Event-Driven Architecture (Zero Polling)**
- **File:** `knowledge/fix-process-polling-to-osc133.md`
- Replace polling with OSC 133 shell integration
- `terminal:command-started` / `terminal:command-finished` IPC events
- Use `terminal:getCommandState` for memory-based status (zero syscalls)

**B. Safe Input for Large Prompts (fix-pty-buffer-overflow.md)**
- Chunked write: 1KB chunks with 10ms delays
- Bracketed paste mode: `\x1b` ... `\x1b[201~`
- Applies automatically to data > 1024 bytes

**C. CWD Tracking (fact-osc7-cwd.md)**
- Shell sends OSC 7 on `cd`: `\e]7;file://localhost$PWD\a`
- No syscalls needed—shell integration provides mutable `cwd`
- Used for script discovery, tab initialization

**D. Markdown Rendering Pipeline**
- **Inline code fix (fix-markdown-inline-code.md):** Check `node?.parent?.tagName !== 'pre'` to detect inline vs block
- **Hydration fix (fix-markdown-hydration.md):** Use `react-virtuoso` for smooth scrolling
- **Pasted blocks (clipboard-tools.md):** `:::pasted` syntax for collapsible sections

**E. Layering Pattern (fix-layering-pattern.md)**
- React Portals for top-level UI (FileExplorer, modals)
- Layering pattern for terminal-overlaid UI (Scroll button, Restart Zone):
  ```tsx
  <div className="absolute inset-0">
    <div ref={terminalRef} className="absolute inset-0" />
    <div className="absolute inset-0 pointer-events-none z-10">
      <button className="pointer-events-auto">↓</button>
    </div>
  </div>
  ```

**F. Data Persistence Strategy (fix-data-persistence.md)**
- **Session State (SQLite):** `app_state` table, debounced 300ms
- **Tab Metadata (SQLite):** Debounced 500ms
- **Emergency Save:** `ipcRenderer.sendSync` on `beforeunload`
- **Interrupted State:** Stored in JSON tab metadata

**G. Title Bar Interaction (fix-titlebar-layered-drag.md)**
- Parent always `WebkitAppRegion: 'drag'`
- Child elements always `WebkitAppRegion: 'no-drag'`
- Use `onMouseDown` on parent (works during drag)
- Check `e.target === e.currentTarget` for double-click on containers

**H. Terminal Stability**
- Canvas renderer (not WebGL) due to context limits and warm-up latency
- Write buffer (10ms flush delay) prevents Ink TUI jitter
- Font loading block (`font-display: block`) prevents metrics misalignment
- Async `execAsync` (never `execSync`) for all system calls
- ResizeObserver with `activeRef` prevents stale closure bugs

**I. Selection & Multi-Selection (fact-selection-model.md)**
- `selectedTabIds` array in store
- Color indicator shows only on active tab (priority over multi-select highlight)
- Context menu adapts: hide Rename/Color on multi-select, show "Close X Tabs"

🤖 CLAUDE:
<thinking>
I see the issue. The context menu closes via `document.addEventListener('click', handleClick)` - a document-level click listener. But the terminal (xterm.js) uses a canvas element that captures mouse events and may not propagate them to the document level consistently.

The fix: change `click` to `mousedown` for closing the context menu, since `mousedown` fires before the terminal canvas can swallow the event. This is a common pattern for context menus.

Also, I need to add the green dot indicat...[truncated]
</thinking>

🤖 CLAUDE:
Вижу проблему с закрытием — `document.addEventListener('click')` не всегда ловит клик по терминалу (canvas xterm.js перехватывает). Нужно `mousedown` вместо `click`. Плюс добавлю стикер к Scripts.

🤖 CLAUDE:
Да, можно и нужно. Логика везде одна, контент — разный. Вот как бы я это разделил:

### Хук `useCmdHoverPopover<T>()`

Вся стейт-машина в одном месте:
- CMD tracking (keydown/keyup/blur)
- `hoveredItem: { id: T, rect: DOMRect } | null`
- `isPinned` state
- Bridge timeout (150ms)
- Cleanup on unmount

Возвращает:
```ts
{
  isCmdPressed,
  hoveredItem,     // { id, rect } | null
  isVisible,       // isCmdPressed || isPinned
  triggerProps(id), // → { onMouseEnter, onMouseLeave } для карточки
  popoverProps,    // → { onMouseEnter, onMouseLeave } для попвера
}
```

### Утилита `getPopoverPosition(rect, preferBelow?)`

Чистая функция: принимает `DOMRect`, возвращает `{ style, maxHeight }` — smart positioning (выше/ниже в зависимости от пространства).

### Компонент `<CmdHoverPopover>`

Тонкая обёртка для рендера:
```tsx
<CmdHoverPopover popoverProps={popoverProps} rect={hoveredItem.rect}>
  {/* любой контент — MarkdownEditor, метаданные, кнопки */}
</CmdHoverPopover>
```

Внутри: `fixed`, `z-[100]`, `boxShadow`, `border`, smart positioning. Контент — через `children`.

### Итого

- **Хук** — вся логика (CMD, hover, pinning, timeout)
- **Позиционирование** — утилита
- **Обёртка** — стили контейнера
- **Контент** — каждый caller передаёт свой через children

Три файла (TabBar, ProjectHome, Dashboard) сократятся до ~5 строк каждый вместо ~40. При этом контент попвера полностью свободный — MarkdownEditor, кнопки, метаданные — всё на стороне вызывающего кода.

Делать?

  редактора и так далее, но сама логика типа псевдоэлемент, который перекрывает моменты, когда у нас курсор двигается по         
  простому пространству и так далее, а вся эта логика по сути одинаковая. Как тут будет архитектурнее, правильно сделать?            
                                                                                                                                   
⏺ Да, можно и нужно. Логика везде одна, контент — разный. Вот как бы я это разделил:                                                 
                                                                                                                                   
  Хук useCmdHoverPopover<T>()                                                                                                        
   
  Вся стейт-машина в одном месте:                                                                                                    
  - CMD tracking (keydown/keyup/blur)                                                                                              
  - hoveredItem: { id: T, rect: DOMRect } | null                                                                                   
  - isPinned state
  - Bridge timeout (150ms)
  - Cleanup on unmount

  Возвращает:
  {
    isCmdPressed,
    hoveredItem,     // { id, rect } | null
    isVisible,       // isCmdPressed || isPinned
    triggerProps(id), // → { onMouseEnter, onMouseLeave } для карточки
    popoverProps,    // → { onMouseEnter, onMouseLeave } для попвера
  }

  Утилита getPopoverPosition(rect, preferBelow?)

  Чистая функция: принимает DOMRect, возвращает { style, maxHeight } — smart positioning (выше/ниже в зависимости от пространства).

  Компонент <CmdHoverPopover>

  Тонкая обёртка для рендера:
  <CmdHoverPopover popoverProps={popoverProps} rect={hoveredItem.rect}>
    {/* любой контент — MarkdownEditor, метаданные, кнопки */}
  </CmdHoverPopover>

  Внутри: fixed, z-[100], boxShadow, border, smart positioning. Контент — через children.

  Итого

  - Хук — вся логика (CMD, hover, pinning, timeout)
  - Позиционирование — утилита
  - Обёртка — стили контейнера
  - Контент — каждый caller передаёт свой через children

  Три файла (TabBar, ProjectHome, Dashboard) сократятся до ~5 строк каждый вместо ~40. При этом контент попвера полностью свободный —
   MarkdownEditor, кнопки, метаданные — всё на стороне вызывающего кода.

## Summary of Documentation Review

Я проверил файлы: `/Users/fedor/Desktop/custom-terminal/docs/architecture.md`, `/Users/fedor/Desktop/custom-terminal/docs/main-feature.md`, и 23 файла из папки `/Users/fedor/Desktop/custom-terminal/docs/knowledge/`.

### Architecture Overview (docs/architecture.md)

The **Noted Terminal** is a custom Electron-based terminal emulator that integrates deeply with AI agents (Claude Code, Gemini CLI). Key architectural components:

1. **Process Model**: Main process manages node-pty terminal sessions, SQLite database, and filesystem. Renderer process is React 19 UI that communicates via typed IPC. Introduces `activeArea` concept ('projects' | 'workspace') for context-aware hotkey interpretation.

2. **Project Instance Model**: Projects are now entities with unique IDs (not just paths). Supports multiple instances of the same directory path, each with independent tabs, notes, and AI history.

3. **Terminal Integration**: Uses xterm.js with Canvas renderer. Implements:
   - **OSC 7** for reactive CWD tracking (shell sends directory changes instead of polling)
   - **OSC 133** for event-driven process status (no polling via pgrep/ps)
   - **Shell Integration** with custom .zshrc/.bashrc in app support directory
   - **Safe Write** (chunked) for large prompts (>4KB)
   - **Claude Sniper & Gemini Sniper** for capturing session IDs via fs.watch

4. **Rendering & Styling**:
   - Tailwind v4 with @tailwindcss/vite plugin for instant HMR
   - Canvas-based terminal (no WebGL to avoid context limits)
   - Inline styles for dynamic colors (Tailwind can't generate arbitrary values at runtime)
   - Custom markdown renderer with hydration fixes

5. **Critical Rules**:
   - **NO execSync** - use execAsync for system calls
   - **NO polling** via pgrep/ps - use OSC 133 events or memory state
   - **Escape $** in template literals for Vite (fix-main-process-escaping.md)
   - **Persistence**: Tab state (color, commandType, CWD, AI session IDs) saved to SQLite

### Main Features (docs/main-feature.md)

Six major user flows:
1. **Project Navigation** - Tab-based project switching, Dashboard, History (LRU), Bookmarks, Home View
2. **Terminal Management** - Scripts runner, Cross-project drag, Timeline navigation, RestartZone
3. **AI Research** - Context menu research, clipboard analysis, custom paste format
4. **Sync & Export** - Claude session export (code stripping), Update Docs flow, Multi-tab selection
5. **Persistence** - All state saved; Interrupted Overlay for resuming broken sessions
6. **Notes & Time Machine** - Markdown notes with Cmd+E fullscreen editor; Gemini rollback to any message

### Knowledge Base (23 files)

**Terminal & Performance Issues:**
- `fix-ui-stability.md` - Comprehensive collection: Write buffering (Ink TUI jitter), persistent terminals, font loading, tabs display conflicts, hover conflicts, system zoom interception, toast positioning, Event Loop protection, Canvas vs WebGL decision, font rendering, background throttling
- `fix-process-polling-to-osc133.md` - Eliminated sysmond CPU overload (334% → 0%) by replacing polling with event-driven architecture
- `fix-terminal-colors.md` - COLORTERM and LANG environment variables for truecolor and UTF-8
- `fix-terminal-resizing.md` - Use refs to avoid stale closures in ResizeObserver callbacks
- `fact-osc7-cwd.md` - Shell Integration pattern: dynamic shell config with OSC 7 sequences

**AI Session Management:**
- `fix-interrupted-overlay-persistence.md` - Two-flag system: `wasInterrupted` + `overlayDismissed` with lifecycle management
- `fix-gemini-id-capture.md` - Sniper 2.0: dynamic CWD hashing, long-lived watcher (5min), JSON parsing
- `fix-gemini-true-fork.md` - Clone session files physically and patch sessionId field instead of using `-r` resume
- `fix-ai-ui-flicker.md` - Immediate ID injection into tab options to prevent race conditions
- `fix-jsonl-backtrace.md` - Backtrace algorithm for filtering canceled (Undo) branches in Claude JSONL logs
- `fix-sniper-dual-method.md` (mentioned in architecture) - fs.watch + polling (1s fallback) for Claude session capture

**Styling & Layout:**
- `fix-tailwind-v4-source.md` - Use @tailwindcss/vite plugin for auto-scanning dependencies
- `fix-markdown-hydration.md` - Custom `<p>` renderer to replace with `<div>` when containing block elements
- `fix-markdown-inline-code.md` - Detect inline vs block code by checking parent tagName
- `fix-markdown-editor-recreation.md` - Avoid literal arrays/objects in default props; use stable constants
- `fix-titlebar-layered-drag.md` - Layered cake pattern: drag parent + no-drag interactive child
- `fix-interactive-hover-zones.md` - Invisible bridge for smooth mouse transitions between triggers and portals
- `fix-layout-clipping.md` - Use relative sizing (w-full/flex-1) in nested components, not fixed widths

**Data & Exports:**
- `fix-claude-clean-export.md` - Transform raw JSONL to compact Markdown: strip code dumps, use emoji markers, truncate thinking
- `fix-data-persistence.md` - Debounced saves (300-500ms), SQLite for app_state, JSON for tab metadata, syncronous save on beforeunload
- `fix-tab-rename-on-restart.md` - Persist `command_type` to SQLite to prevent auto-rename after restart

**Model & Selection:**
- `fact-selection-model.md` - Multi-select tabs with Shift/Cmd+Click, bulk actions, color indicator only on active
- `fix-project-instances.md` - UUID generation: base64(path)[:20] + timestamp + random, supports multiple instances per path

**Other:**
- `fix-pty-buffer-overflow.md` - Chunked write (1KB + 10ms delay) + Bracketed Paste Mode for large inputs
- `fix-main-process-escaping.md` - Escape $ in template literals for Vite
- `fix-layering-pattern.md` - React Portals for global UI; stacked `absolute` layers for terminal-relative UI; pointer-events management
- `fix-ai-ui-flicker.md` - Immediate injection pattern for session IDs

### Technical Stack Highlights
- **Frontend:** React 19, Vite, TypeScript, Tailwind v4
- **Terminal:** xterm.js with Canvas renderer (no WebGL)
- **Backend:** Node.js, node-pty, SQLite
- **Shell Integration:** Custom .zshrc/.bashrc with OSC 7 and OSC 133
- **AI Integration:** Event-driven architecture (no polling); fs.watch for session capture; JSONL parsing with backtrace algorithm

### Critical Design Decisions
1. **Projects as Entities** - Multiple instances of same path possible
2. **Event-Driven** - OSC 133 for process status, OSC 7 for CWD (zero syscalls for monitoring)
3. **Canvas Rendering** - Eliminates WebGL context limit and warm-up lag
4. **Debounced Persistence** - IPC and disk I/O optimized
5. **Immediate ID Injection** - Prevents UI flicker during tab creation/recovery
6. **Safe Write** - Chunked PTY input to prevent buffer overflow
7. **Backtrace Algorithm** - Correctly handles Undo branches in JSONL logs</result>

🤖 CLAUDE:
Готово. Проблема была в том, что `document.addEventListener('mousedown', handleClose)` безусловно закрывал контекстное меню при любом mousedown, не проверяя, кликнули ли внутри самого меню. React'овский `onMouseDown stopPropagation` мог не перехватить нативный listener на document из-за event delegation.

Фикс:
1. В close handler добавил проверку `e.target.closest('[data-tab-context-menu]')` — если клик внутри меню, не закрываем
2. Добавил атрибут `data-tab-context-menu` на div контекстного меню (он уже был в проверке selection clearing, но не был установлен на элементе)
